msg:I originally planned to live in Shangri-La, and then found out that Manhattan was newly opened this year, so I chose Manhattan. The price/performance ratio is really high, the room type is good, the sanitation is great, and the service is good. The only thing that needs to be strengthened is that the mobile phone is out of power, and the hotel does not have a charger or charging cable. Others are very good and highly recommended.
